Compare analogous <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gebärmutter</i>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baarmoeder.html>baarmoeder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">womb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hals.html>hals</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly attested as early as the 18th century.
</p>

***baas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a> (550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">master of a household, friend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*baso</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">uncle, kinsman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baswô</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">bās</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">supervisor, <a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:bas.html>bas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; possibly also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">basa</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"father's sister, cousin"; gt; German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Base</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">aunt, cousin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazen.html>bazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baasje.html>baasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazin.html>bazin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boss, chief, superior</li>
<li>employer, manager</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> strong or tough guy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">video games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boss</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crack, master, expert at something</li>

***babbelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:babbelen.html>babbelen</a> (8240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:babbelen.html>babbelen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*babbalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*babalōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:babbelen.html>babbelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chatter, to chit-chat, to talk casually</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nibble, to bite on something</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kletsen.html>kletsen</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a> (30074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babysitter.html>babysitter</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">babysits</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">babysitting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">babysat</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To watch or tend someone else's child for a period of time, often for money.
<dl><dd><i>My daughter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>babysitting</b> for the <a href = vnd.unilang:morgans.html>Morgans</a> at number ten, who are going out on a date night.</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> need someone to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b> our children while <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> go to the <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> May 27,  Nathan Rabin,  “TV: Review: THE SIMPSONS (CLASSIC): “New Kid On The Block” (season 4, episode 8; originally aired 11/12/1992)”, in  <cite>The Onion AV Club</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.avclub.com/articles/new-kid-on-the-block,75341/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Bart eventually <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b> while <a href = vnd.unilang:homer.html>Homer</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:marge.html>Marge</a> eat at the Sea <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a>’s all-you-can-eat seafood joint, The Frying <a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>Dutchman</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To watch or attend anything or anyone unnecessarily closely; to have to help or coax too much.
<dl><dd><i>He left <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b> the new guy while he got some work done.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2016</b>, Christopher Vasey, <i>Nazi Intelligence Operations in Non-Occupied Territories</i> (page 175)
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> observed by the FBI personnel assigned to “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysit.html>babysit</a></b>” <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> Tricycle that his egregiously excessive spending <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> causing unwanted attention <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sitter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A person who cares for one or more <a href = vnd.unilang:babies.html>babies</a> or children for a short period of time in place of their legal <a href = vnd.unilang:guardians.html>guardians</a>.
<dl><dd><i>My neighbor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:babysitter.html>babysitter</a></b> for other moms' children.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***baccarat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a> (55085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">baccara</i> <span class="defdate">[19th c.]</span>, likely named after the French town <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baccarat" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Baccarat"><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>Baccarat</a></a> (noted for glassmaking) in Grand Est, of ultimately unclear and debated origin <span class="defdate">[1291?]</span>. If by some <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*Bacchara</i>, the town <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possibly named from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Bacchi</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ara.html>ara</a></i> ("altar of Bacchus"; the original pagan reference of the name <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a>), name of an ancient Roman <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">castellum</i>, of which there <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> a relic called the "Tower of Bacha" on the heights of Deneuvre, from whence <a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>Baccarat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an ancient suburb. Other <a href = vnd.unilang:hypotheses.html>hypotheses</a> have also <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> suggested, including descent from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span>.
</p><p>Probably linked to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proven%C3%A7al_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Provençal dialect">Provençal</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">baccara</i>, although if the town etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> correct, this may present some geographic difficulty.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Au_bac.jpg/220px-Au_bac.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="266" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Au_bac.jpg/330px-Au_bac.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Au_bac.jpg/440px-Au_bac.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1213" data-file-height="1468" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A game of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></b>, illustrated from 1897 by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albert_Guillaume" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Albert Guillaume">Albert Guillaume</a>.</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A card game resembling <a href = vnd.unilang:chemin.html>chemin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> fer with many forms <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> usually entailing the player(s) betting against two or three hands <a href = vnd.unilang:dealt.html>dealt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> also bearing some similarities to blackjack.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>By far, the most common style played <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:punto.html>punto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banco.html>banco</a></i>, where the closest total value to 9 between a pair of cards by "Player" or "Banker" wins.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:baccarat.html>baccarat</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p>

***backgammon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> (32057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamen.html>gamen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamen.html>gamen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">amusement, game</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/150px-Backgammon_lg.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="100" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/225px-Backgammon_lg.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/300px-Backgammon_lg.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> board shown in starting position.</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">backgammons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A board game for two players in which each <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> 15 stones which move between 24 triangular points <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the roll of a pair of dice; the object <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to move all of one's pieces around, and bear them off the board.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A victory in the game when the <a href = vnd.unilang:loser.html>loser</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not borne off a stone, and still <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> one or more stones in the winner's inner home row or on the <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gammon</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">backgammons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backgammoning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backgammoned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To win at a <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> game with the opponent having one or more pieces in the winner’s inner home row or on the <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> triktrak <a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleid.html>afgeleid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bordspel.html>bordspel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:personen.html>personen</a></li></ol>
<p><br />
</p>
</body> 
***backhand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a> (32803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hand</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">backhands</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">tennis</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <a href = vnd.unilang:stroken.html>stroke</a> made across the chest from the off-hand side to the racquet hand side; a <a href = vnd.unilang:stroken.html>stroke</a> during which the back of the hand <a href = vnd.unilang:faces.html>faces</a> the shot.</li>
<li>Handwriting that leans to the left</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Ultimate <a href = vnd.unilang:frisbee.html>Frisbee</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the standard throw; a throw during which the disc begins on the off-hand side and travels across the chest to be released from the opposite side.</li>
<li>The reverse side of the human hand.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">surfing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the hand towards the back of the board.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">backhands</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backhanding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">backhanded</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to execute a <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stroken.html>stroke</a> or throw</li>
<li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:slap.html>slap</a> with the back of one's hand</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">handwriting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of any left slanting handwriting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of strokes or throws</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In the <a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a> style</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ice hockey</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a play that uses the back side of the hockey stick
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He scored on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b> shot.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:backhand.html>backhand</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/(<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(sport)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterwaartse.html>achterwaartse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> bijv. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tennisracket.html>tennisracket</a>

***baden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baden.html>baden</a> (10202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bāden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bathon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baþōną</i>.

***badkamer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamer</a> (1999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bad</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamers.html>badkamers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bathroom</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In English, <i>bathroom</i> may mean a room with only a <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:badkamer.html>badkamer</a></i> always refers to a room with a bath and/or a shower (and possibly a <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>).
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:baggeren.html>baggeren</a></i>. ***bajes.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bajes.html>bajes</a> (8865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">בית</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:bajes.html>bajes</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">בית</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">báyit</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bajes.html>bajes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bajes.html>bajesen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bajes.html>bajesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bake</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baec</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meat from the back of a pig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">back, rear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baką</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">back</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i>. Etymologically related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakboord.html>bakboord</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a></i>.
</p>

***bakboord.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakboord.html>bakboord</a> (8468)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boord.html>boord</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">board</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because the pilot <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> formerly located on the starboard, thereby turning his back to the other side.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***baken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baken.html>baken</a> (8769)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:baken.html>baken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">bāken</i>. Displaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bōkan</i>. Both forms originate from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baukną</i>.
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any urban myth or unfounded, unreliable story</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fight, to brawl <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to engage in physical combat</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[late 17th <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 20th c.]</span></li></ol>

***bakken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a> (4182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">backen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:baken.html>baken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bakkan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bakan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bakaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰeh₃g-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pan-fry</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pan-fry</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> The distinction between <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:braden.html>braden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> somewhat unclear and depending on idiolect. The general word for pan-frying <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i>, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:braden.html>braden</a></i> may alternatively be used with meat. Many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> use <i><a href = vnd.unilang:braden.html>braden</a></i> chiefly in the sense of “to roast, to grill”.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">backer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bakar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*baker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bakārijaz</i>.

***bakkerij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakkerij.html>bakkerij</a> (12953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Or alternatively, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>bakker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also the usage notes at <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bakery</i>, and German and Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bäckerei</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bakery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakpoeder.html>bakpoeder</a> (58130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakken.html>bakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bake, fry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “teenage girl” <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Backfisch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakvis.html>bakvis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakvissen.html>bakvissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakvisje.html>bakvisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pubescent girl, connoting giggliness and fangirlism.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fish cooked by frying (rather then boiling etc.), referring either a culinary dish or a species usually thus prepared.
<ul><li><b>1863</b>, von Ehrenkreutz, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebber</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hengelen.html>hengelen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:volledig.html>Volledig</a> handboek ten <a href = vnd.unilang:dienste.html>dienste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hengelaars.html>hengelaars</a></i>, tr. from German, H. C. A. <a href = vnd.unilang:campagne.html>Campagne</a> (publ.), page 82.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Hesseling] <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezonde.html>gezonde</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <b>bakvisch</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***bal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a> (943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*balluz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballen.html>ballen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balletje.html>balletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a ball or any object with such a shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> testicle, <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pass, shot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>Lekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:balletje.html>balletje</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Nice pass/shot!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">toff</span>, posh person</li></ol>

***balalaika.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balalaika.html>balalaika</a> (109422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">балала́йка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balalájka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:balalaika.html>balalaika</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">balalaikas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">balalaiki</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A plucked stringed instrument with a triangular body, short neck and three <a href = vnd.unilang:strings.html>strings</a>, of Russian origin.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:balalaika.html>balalaika</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***balans.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balans.html>balans</a> (4851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">balanse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">balance</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bilanx</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balans.html>balans</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balansen.html>balansen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balans.html>balansje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>balance, scales for weighing</li>
<li>equilibrium</li>
<li>balance sheet</li>
<li>type of bridge with counterweight</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***baldrick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a> (12568)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">baldricks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A broad <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>, sometimes richly ornamented, worn <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> one shoulder, across the breast, and under the opposite arm; less properly, any <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>.
<ul><li><b>1400?</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Gawain and the Green Knight</i>, line 2485.:
<dl><dd>And the bright green <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a> on his body he <a href = vnd.unilang:boren.html>bore</a>, oblique, like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></b>, bound at his side below his left shoulder, laced in a knot...</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1598</b>, William Shakespeare, <i>Much Ado About Nothing</i>, Act I, Scene I, line 238:
<dl><dd>That a woman conceiv'd <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, I thank her; that she <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> up, I likewise give her most humble <a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a>; but that I will have a rechate winded in my forehead, or hang my <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a> in an invisible <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></b>, all women shall <a href = vnd.unilang:pardon.html>pardon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1800?</b>, Alfred, Lord Tennyson, <i>The Lady Of Shalott</i>, part III, verse 2:
<dl><dd>And from his blazoned <b><a href = vnd.unilang:baldrick.html>baldrick</a></b> slung, a mighty silver <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a> hung...</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1786</b>,  Francis Grose,  <cite>A Treatise on Ancient Armour and <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>Weapons</a></cite>, page 33:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The sword <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> carried in a <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a> of buff or other leather girded round the body, or thrown <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the right shoulder, these shoulder belts <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> called <b>baudricks</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>
